  [user_task_description] # Requirements Document for 'RealEstate' Web Application  ## 1. Objective Develop a comprehensive web application named 'RealEstate' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse property listings, search by location and price, view property details, submit inquiries, and manage favorite properties. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.  ## 2. Language The required development language for the 'RealEstate' application is Python.  ## 3. Page Design  The 'RealEstate' web application will consist of the following eight pages:  ### 1. Dashboard Page - **Page Title**: Real Estate Dashboard - **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured properties, recent listings, and quick navigation to all functionalities. - **Elements**:   - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.   - **ID: featured-properties** - Type: Div - Display of featured property recommendations.   - **ID: browse-properties-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to property search page.   - **ID: my-inquiries-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to inquiries page.   - **ID: my-favorites-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to favorites page.  ### 2. Property Search Page - **Page Title**: Property Search - **Overview**: A page displaying all available properties with advanced search and filter capabilities. - **Elements**:   - **ID: search-page** - Type: Div - Container for the search page.   - **ID: location-input** - Type: Input - Field to search properties by location/city.   - **ID: price-range-min** - Type: Input (number) - Field to set minimum price filter.   - **ID: price-range-max** - Type: Input (number) - Field to set maximum price filter.   - **ID: property-type-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by property type (House, Apartment, Condo, Land).   - **ID: properties-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying property cards with image, location, price, and beds/baths.   - **ID: view-property-button-{property_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view property details (each property card has this).  ### 3. Property Details Page - **Page Title**: Property Details - **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific property. - **Elements**:   - **ID: property-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the property details page.   - **ID: property-address** - Type: H1 - Display property address.   - **ID: property-price** - Type: Div - Display property price.   - **ID: property-description** - Type: Div - Display property description.   - **ID: property-features** - Type: Div - Display property features (beds, baths, square footage).   - **ID: add-to-favorites-button** - Type: Button - Button to add property to favorites.   - **ID: submit-inquiry-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit inquiry for property.  ### 4. Property Inquiry Page - **Page Title**: Submit Property Inquiry - **Overview**: A page for users to submit inquiries for properties they are interested in. - **Elements**:   - **ID: inquiry-page** - Type: Div - Container for the inquiry page.   - **ID: select-property** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select property for inquiry.   - **ID: inquiry-name** - Type: Input - Field to input customer name.   - **ID: inquiry-email** - Type: Input (email) - Field to input customer email.   - **ID: inquiry-phone** - Type: Input (tel) - Field to input customer phone.   - **ID: inquiry-message** - Type: Textarea - Field to write inquiry message.   - **ID: submit-inquiry-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit inquiry.  ### 5. My Inquiries Page - **Page Title**: My Inquiries - **Overview**: A page displaying all submitted inquiries and their status. - **Elements**:   - **ID: inquiries-page** - Type: Div - Container for the inquiries page.   - **ID: inquiries-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying inquiries with property, date, status, and contact info.   - **ID: inquiry-status-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (All, Pending, Contacted, Resolved).   - **ID: delete-inquiry-button-{inquiry_id}** - Type: Button - Button to delete inquiry (each inquiry has this).   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 6. My Favorites Page - **Page Title**: My Favorite Properties - **Overview**: A page displaying all properties added to favorites. - **Elements**:   - **ID: favorites-page** - Type: Div - Container for the favorites page.   - **ID: favorites-list** - Type: Div - List of all favorite properties with address, price, and action buttons.   - **ID: remove-from-favorites-button-{property_id}** - Type: Button - Button to remove property from favorites (each property has this).   - **ID: view-property-button-{property_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view property details (each property has this).   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 7. Agent Directory Page - **Page Title**: Real Estate Agents - **Overview**: A page displaying all real estate agents and their contact information. - **Elements**:   - **ID: agents-page** - Type: Div - Container for the agents page.   - **ID: agents-list** - Type: Div - List of all agents with photo, name, specialization, and contact info.   - **ID: agent-search** - Type: Input - Field to search agents by name.   - **ID: contact-agent-button-{agent_id}** - Type: Button - Button to contact agent (each agent has this).   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 8. Locations Page - **Page Title**: Featured Locations - **Overview**: A page displaying popular locations with property count and details. - **Elements**:   - **ID: locations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the locations page.   - **ID: locations-list** - Type: Div - List of all locations with name, property count, and average price.   - **ID: view-location-button-{location_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view properties in location (each location has this).   - **ID: location-sort** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to sort locations (By Name, By Properties Count, By Average Price).   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ## 4. Data Storage  The 'RealEstate' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:  ### 1. Properties Data - **File Name**: `properties.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   property_id|address|location|price|property_type|bedrooms|bathrooms|square_feet|description|agent_id|status   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|123 Oak Street|Downtown|450000|House|3|2|2500|Beautiful family home with large yard|101|Available   2|456 Park Avenue|Midtown|350000|Apartment|2|1.5|1200|Modern apartment with city view|102|Available   3|789 Elm Road|Suburb|280000|Condo|2|2|1500|Cozy condo in quiet neighborhood|101|Sold   ```  ### 2. Locations Data - **File Name**: `locations.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   location_id|location_name|region|average_price|property_count|description   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Downtown|Central|425000|45|Urban area with business district   2|Midtown|Central|380000|38|Mixed residential and commercial zone   3|Suburb|Outskirts|295000|52|Family-friendly residential area   ```  ### 3. Property Inquiries Data - **File Name**: `inquiries.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   inquiry_id|property_id|customer_name|customer_email|customer_phone|message|inquiry_date|status   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|John Smith|john@email.com|555-1234|Interested in viewing this weekend|2025-01-15|Pending   2|2|Sarah Johnson|sarah@email.com|555-5678|Can we schedule a showing?|2025-01-16|Contacted   3|1|Mike Davis|mike@email.com|555-9012|What is the lowest offer?|2025-01-17|Resolved   ```  ### 4. Favorite Properties Data - **File Name**: `favorites.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   favorite_id|property_id|added_date   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|2025-01-10   2|2|2025-01-12   3|3|2025-01-14   ```  ### 5. Real Estate Agents Data - **File Name**: `agents.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   agent_id|agent_name|specialization|email|phone|properties_sold   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   101|Robert Wilson|Residential Properties|robert@email.com|555-0001|125   102|Emily Chen|Commercial Real Estate|emily@email.com|555-0002|89   103|James Martinez|Luxury Homes|james@email.com|555-0003|67   ```

Objective\n\nDevelop a comprehensive design specification for a fully functional local file-based RealEstate web application where users can browse property listings, search by location and price, view property details, submit property inquiries, and manage favorite properties. Flask Routes Specification\n\n### 3.1 Dashboard\n- URL: `/`\n- Methods: GET\n- Description: Main landing page showing featured properties, navigation links to search, favorites, inquiries, agents, and locations.\n- Context Variables:\n  - `featured_properties` - list of featured property dicts\n\n---\n\n### 3.2 Search Properties\n- URL: `/search`\n- Methods: GET, POST\n- Description: Page with search form to filter properties by price range (min/max), property type, location.\n- Context Variables:\n  - `properties` - list of filtered property dicts\n  - `filters` - dict of submitted filter criteria\n\n---\n\n### 3.3 Property Details\n- URL: `/property/<property_id>`\n- Methods: GET\n- Description: Display detailed property information, with buttons to add to favorites and submit inquiry.\n- Context Variables:\n  - `property` - dict of property details\n\n---\n\n### 3.4 Submit Inquiry\n- URL: `/inquiry` or `/inquiry/<property_id>`\n- Methods: GET, POST\n- Description: Form page to submit an inquiry about a property or a general inquiry.\n- Context Variables:\n  - `property` (optional) - dict of property details\n\n---\n\n### 3.5 View Inquiries\n- URL: `/inquiries`\n- Methods: GET\n- Description: List all submitted inquiries with filter by status.\n- Context Variables:\n  - `inquiries` - list of inquiry dicts\n  - `status_filter` - current filter status\n\n---\n\n### 3.6 Favorites Page\n- URL: `/favorites`\n- Methods: GET\n- Description: Displays favorite properties, with buttons to remove favorites and view property details.\n- Context Variables:\n  - `favorites` - list of favorite property dicts\n\n---\n\n### 3.7 Agents Page\n- URL: `/agents`\n- Methods: GET\n- Description: List all real estate agents with contact buttons.\n- Context Variables:\n  - `agents` - list of agents dicts\n\n---\n\n### 3.8 Locations Page\n- URL: `/locations`\n- Methods: GET\n- Description: List locations with average price and counts. Buttons to view location properties.\n- Context Variables:\n  - `locations` - list of location dicts\n\n---\n\n## 4. HTML Templates Outline\n\n### 4.1 Base Layout\n- Navigation menu with links to Dashboard, Search, Favorites, Inquiries, Agents, Locations.\n\n### 4.2 Dashboard Page\n- Container div with id `dashboard-container`.\n- Section showing featured properties each with button linking to property details.\n- Buttons:\n  - `browse-properties-button` - navigates to search.\n  - `my-favorites-button` - navigates to favorites page.\n\n### 4.3 Search Page\n- Search form with input fields:\n  - `price-range-min` (number input)\n  - `price-range-max` (number input)\n  - `property-type-filter` (dropdown)\n  - `location-filter` (dropdown)\n- Search results displayed as property cards.\n- Each card contains:\n  - Image, address, price, bedrooms, bathrooms.\n  - Button linking to property details.\n\n### 4.4 Property Details Page\n- Container div `property-details-page`.\n- Display property price `property-price`.\n- Description div `property-description`.\n- Button `add-favorite-button` to add property to favorites.\n- Button `submit-inquiry-button` to open inquiry form.\n\n### 4.5 Inquiry Form Page\n- Container `inquiry-page`.\n- Form inputs:\n  - `inquiry-name` (text)\n  - `inquiry-email` (email)\n  - `inquiry-phone` (tel)\n  - `inquiry-message` (textarea)\n  - Dropdown to select property if inquiry is general.\n- Submit button `submit-inquiry-button`.\n\n### 4.6 Inquiries List Page\n- Container `inquiries-page`.\n- Table `inquiries-table` listing inquiries with columns for property, customer, date, and status.\n- Dropdown filter `inquiry-status-filter`.\n- Button per inquiry `delete-inquiry-button-{inquiry_id}`.\n\n### 4.7 Favorites Page\n- Container div `favorites-list`.\n- List favorite properties with buttons:\n  - `remove-from-favorites-button-{property_id}`\n  - `view-property-button-{property_id}`\n- Back button `back-to-dashboard`.\n\n### 4.8 Agents Page\n- Container div `agents-list`.\n- List agents with contact button `contact-agent-button-{agent_id}`.\n- Back button `back-to-dashboard`.\n\n### 4.9 Locations Page\n- Container `locations-page`.\n- List locations with summary info.\n- Buttons `view-location-button-{location_id}` for viewing location details.\n- Sort dropdown by average price `location-sort-dropdown`.\n- Back to dashboard button.\n\n---\n\n## 5. Data File Schemas\n\n### 5.1 Properties (`properties.txt`)\nFormat:\n```\nproperty_id|address|location|price|property_type|bedrooms|bathrooms|square_feet|description|agent_id|status\n```\n\n### 5.2 Locations (`locations.txt`)\nFormat:\n```\nlocation_id|location_name|region|average_price|property_count|description\n```\n\n### 5.3 Inquiries (`inquiries.txt`)\nFormat:\n```\ninquiry_id|property_id|customer_name|customer_email|customer_phone|message|inquiry_date|status\n```\n\n### 5.4 Favorites (`favorites.txt`)\nFormat:\n```\nfavorite_id|property_id|added_date\n```\n\n### 5.5 Agents (`agents.txt`)\nFormat:\n```\nagent_id|name|agency|email|phone|specialization\n```\n\n---\n\n## 6. Development Notes\n- Use Flask routing to map URLs to functions rendering templates with correct context.\n- Utilize Jinja2 for template rendering with dynamic elements.\n- Load and save data from/to text files with locking to handle concurrency.\n- Maintain consistent ID keys for properties, inquiries, agents, etc.\n- Ensure navigation links are consistent across all pages.\n- No database or external services are used.\n- Implement clear error handling for file I/O issues.\n- Modularize code for maintainability.\n"})

Each card contains:   - Image, address, price, bedrooms, bathrooms.   - Button linking to property details.  ### 4.4 Property Details Page - Container div `property-details-page`. - Display property price `property-price`. - Description div `property-description`. - Button `add-favorite-button` to add property to favorites. - Button `submit-inquiry-button` to open inquiry form.  ### 4.5 Inquiry Form Page - Container `inquiry-page`. - Form inputs:   - `inquiry-name` (text)   - `inquiry-email` (email)   - `inquiry-phone` (tel)   - `inquiry-message` (textarea)   - Dropdown to select property if inquiry is general. - Submit button `submit-inquiry-button`.  ### 4.6 Inquiries List Page - Container `inquiries-page`. - Table `inquiries-table` listing inquiries with columns for property, customer, date, and status. - Dropdown filter `inquiry-status-filter`. - Button per inquiry `delete-inquiry-button-{inquiry_id}`.  ### 4.7 Favorites Page - Container div `favorites-list`. - List favorite properties with buttons:   - `remove-from-favorites-button-{property_id}`   - `view-property-button-{property_id}` - Back button `back-to-dashboard`.  ### 4.8 Agents Page - Container div `agents-list`. - List agents with contact button `contact-agent-button-{agent_id}`. - Back button `back-to-dashboard`.  ### 4.9 Locations Page - Container `locations-page`. - List locations with summary info. - Buttons `view-location-button-{location_id}` for viewing location details. - Sort dropdown by average price `location-sort-dropdown`. - Back to dashboard button.  ---  ## 5. Data File Schemas  ### 5.1 Properties (`properties.txt`) Format: ``` property_id|address|location|price|property_type|bedrooms|bathrooms|square_feet|description|agent_id|status ```  ### 5.2 Locations (`locations.txt`) Format: ``` location_id|location_name|region|average_price|property_count|description ```  ### 5.3 Inquiries (`inquiries.txt`) Format: ``` inquiry_id|property_id|customer_name|customer_email|customer_phone|message|inquiry_date|status ```  ### 5.4 Favorites (`favorites.txt`) Format: ``` favorite_id|property_id|added_date ```  ### 5.5 Agents (`agents.txt`) Format: ``` agent_id|name|agency|email|phone|specialization ```  ---  ## 6. Development Notes - Use Flask routing to map URLs to functions rendering templates with correct context. - Utilize Jinja2 for template rendering with dynamic elements. - Load and save data from/to text files with locking to handle concurrency. - Maintain consistent ID keys for properties, inquiries, agents, etc. - Ensure navigation links are consistent across all pages. - No database or external services are used. - Implement clear error handling for file I/O issues. - Modularize code for maintainability.

# Requirements Document for 'RealEstate' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'RealEstate' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse property listings, search by location and price, view property details, submit inquiries, and manage favorite properties. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'RealEstate' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'RealEstate' web application will consist of the following eight pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Real Estate Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured properties, recent listings, and quick navigation to all functionalities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: featured-properties** - Type: Div - Display of featured property recommendations.
  - **ID: browse-properties-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to property search page.
  - **ID: my-inquiries-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to inquiries page.
  - **ID: my-favorites-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to favorites page.

### 2. Property Search Page
- **Page Title**: Property Search
- **Overview**: A page displaying all available properties with advanced search and filter capabilities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: search-page** - Type: Div - Container for the search page.
  - **ID: location-input** - Type: Input - Field to search properties by location/city.
  - **ID: price-range-min** - Type: Input (number) - Field to set minimum price filter.
  - **ID: price-range-max** - Type: Input (number) - Field to set maximum price filter.
  - **ID: property-type-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by property type (House, Apartment, Condo, Land).
  - **ID: properties-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying property cards with image, location, price, and beds/baths.
  - **ID: view-property-button-{property_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view property details (each property card has this).

### 3. Property Details Page
- **Page Title**: Property Details
- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific property.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: property-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the property details page.
  - **ID: property-address** - Type: H1 - Display property address.
  - **ID: property-price** - Type: Div - Display property price.
  - **ID: property-description** - Type: Div - Display property description.
  - **ID: property-features** - Type: Div - Display property features (beds, baths, square footage).
  - **ID: add-to-favorites-button** - Type: Button - Button to add property to favorites.
  - **ID: submit-inquiry-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit inquiry for property.

### 4. Property Inquiry Page
- **Page Title**: Submit Property Inquiry
- **Overview**: A page for users to submit inquiries for properties they are interested in.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: inquiry-page** - Type: Div - Container for the inquiry page.
  - **ID: select-property** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select property for inquiry.
  - **ID: inquiry-name** - Type: Input - Field to input customer name.
  - **ID: inquiry-email** - Type: Input (email) - Field to input customer email.
  - **ID: inquiry-phone** - Type: Input (tel) - Field to input customer phone.
  - **ID: inquiry-message** - Type: Textarea - Field to write inquiry message.
  - **ID: submit-inquiry-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit inquiry.

### 5. My Inquiries Page
- **Page Title**: My Inquiries
- **Overview**: A page displaying all submitted inquiries and their status.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: inquiries-page** - Type: Div - Container for the inquiries page.
  - **ID: inquiries-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying inquiries with property, date, status, and contact info.
  - **ID: inquiry-status-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (All, Pending, Contacted, Resolved).
  - **ID: delete-inquiry-button-{inquiry_id}** - Type: Button - Button to delete inquiry (each inquiry has this).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 6. My Favorites Page
- **Page Title**: My Favorite Properties
- **Overview**: A page displaying all properties added to favorites.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: favorites-page** - Type: Div - Container for the favorites page.
  - **ID: favorites-list** - Type: Div - List of all favorite properties with address, price, and action buttons.
  - **ID: remove-from-favorites-button-{property_id}** - Type: Button - Button to remove property from favorites (each property has this).
  - **ID: view-property-button-{property_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view property details (each property has this).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 7. Agent Directory Page
- **Page Title**: Real Estate Agents
- **Overview**: A page displaying all real estate agents and their contact information.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: agents-page** - Type: Div - Container for the agents page.
  - **ID: agents-list** - Type: Div - List of all agents with photo, name, specialization, and contact info.
  - **ID: agent-search** - Type: Input - Field to search agents by name.
  - **ID: contact-agent-button-{agent_id}** - Type: Button - Button to contact agent (each agent has this).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 8. Locations Page
- **Page Title**: Featured Locations
- **Overview**: A page displaying popular locations with property count and details.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: locations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the locations page.
  - **ID: locations-list** - Type: Div - List of all locations with name, property count, and average price.
  - **ID: view-location-button-{location_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view properties in location (each location has this).
  - **ID: location-sort** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to sort locations (By Name, By Properties Count, By Average Price).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'RealEstate' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. Properties Data
- **File Name**: `properties.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  property_id|address|location|price|property_type|bedrooms|bathrooms|square_feet|description|agent_id|status
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|123 Oak Street|Downtown|450000|House|3|2|2500|Beautiful family home with large yard|101|Available
  2|456 Park Avenue|Midtown|350000|Apartment|2|1.5|1200|Modern apartment with city view|102|Available
  3|789 Elm Road|Suburb|280000|Condo|2|2|1500|Cozy condo in quiet neighborhood|101|Sold
  ```

### 2. Locations Data
- **File Name**: `locations.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  location_id|location_name|region|average_price|property_count|description
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Downtown|Central|425000|45|Urban area with business district
  2|Midtown|Central|380000|38|Mixed residential and commercial zone
  3|Suburb|Outskirts|295000|52|Family-friendly residential area
  ```

### 3. Property Inquiries Data
- **File Name**: `inquiries.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  inquiry_id|property_id|customer_name|customer_email|customer_phone|message|inquiry_date|status
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|John Smith|john@email.com|555-1234|Interested in viewing this weekend|2025-01-15|Pending
  2|2|Sarah Johnson|sarah@email.com|555-5678|Can we schedule a showing?|2025-01-16|Contacted
  3|1|Mike Davis|mike@email.com|555-9012|What is the lowest offer?|2025-01-17|Resolved
  ```

### 4. Favorite Properties Data
- **File Name**: `favorites.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  favorite_id|property_id|added_date
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|2025-01-10
  2|2|2025-01-12
  3|3|2025-01-14
  ```

### 5. Real Estate Agents Data
- **File Name**: `agents.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  agent_id|agent_name|specialization|email|phone|properties_sold
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  101|Robert Wilson|Residential Properties|robert@email.com|555-0001|125
  102|Emily Chen|Commercial Real Estate|emily@email.com|555-0002|89
  103|James Martinez|Luxury Homes|james@email.com|555-0003|67
  ```


=== design_spec.md ===
# RealEstate Application Design Specification

## 1. Objective

Develop a comprehensive design specification for a fully functional local file-based RealEstate web application where users can browse property listings, search by location and price, view property details, submit property inquiries, and manage favorite properties. Entirely based on Python Flask backend with local text file data storage.

## 2. Technology Stack
- Backend: Python with Flask
- Frontend: HTML5 with Jinja2 templating
- Data Storage: Local text files

---

## 3. Flask Routes Specification

### 3.1 Dashboard
- URL: `/`
- Methods: GET
- Description: Main landing page showing featured properties, navigation links to search, favorites, inquiries, agents, and locations.
- Context Variables:
  - `featured_properties` - list of featured property dicts

---

### 3.2 Search Properties
- URL: `/search`
- Methods: GET, POST
- Description: Page with search form to filter properties by price range (min/max), property type, location.
- Context Variables:
  - `properties` - list of filtered property dicts
  - `filters` - dict of submitted filter criteria

---

### 3.3 Property Details
- URL: `/property/<property_id>`
- Methods: GET
- Description: Display detailed property information, with buttons to add to favorites and submit inquiry.
- Context Variables:
  - `property` - dict of property details

---

### 3.4 Submit Inquiry
- URL: `/inquiry` or `/inquiry/<property_id>`
- Methods: GET, POST
- Description: Form page to submit an inquiry about a property or a general inquiry.
- Context Variables:
  - `property` (optional) - dict of property details

---

### 3.5 View Inquiries
- URL: `/inquiries`
- Methods: GET
- Description: List all submitted inquiries with filter by status.
- Context Variables:
  - `inquiries` - list of inquiry dicts
  - `status_filter` - current filter status

---

### 3.6 Favorites Page
- URL: `/favorites`
- Methods: GET
- Description: Displays favorite properties, with buttons to remove favorites and view property details.
- Context Variables:
  - `favorites` - list of favorite property dicts

---

### 3.7 Agents Page
- URL: `/agents`
- Methods: GET
- Description: List all real estate agents with contact buttons.
- Context Variables:
  - `agents` - list of agents dicts

---

### 3.8 Locations Page
- URL: `/locations`
- Methods: GET
- Description: List locations with average price and counts. Buttons to view location properties.
- Context Variables:
  - `locations` - list of location dicts

---

## 4. HTML Templates Outline

### 4.1 Base Layout
- Navigation menu with links to Dashboard, Search, Favorites, Inquiries, Agents, Locations.

### 4.2 Dashboard Page
- Container div with id `dashboard-container`.
- Section showing featured properties each with button linking to property details.
- Buttons:
  - `browse-properties-button` - navigates to search.
  - `my-favorites-button` - navigates to favorites page.

### 4.3 Search Page
- Search form with input fields:
  - `price-range-min` (number input)
  - `price-range-max` (number input)
  - `property-type-filter` (dropdown)
  - `location-filter` (dropdown)
- Search results displayed as property cards.
- Each card contains:
  - Image, address, price, bedrooms, bathrooms.
  - Button linking to property details.

### 4.4 Property Details Page
- Container div `property-details-page`.
- Display property price `property-price`.
- Description div `property-description`.
- Button `add-favorite-button` to add property to favorites.
- Button `submit-inquiry-button` to open inquiry form.

### 4.5 Inquiry Form Page
- Container `inquiry-page`.
- Form inputs:
  - `inquiry-name` (text)
  - `inquiry-email` (email)
  - `inquiry-phone` (tel)
  - `inquiry-message` (textarea)
  - Dropdown to select property if inquiry is general.
- Submit button `submit-inquiry-button`.

### 4.6 Inquiries List Page
- Container `inquiries-page`.
- Table `inquiries-table` listing inquiries with columns for property, customer, date, and status.
- Dropdown filter `inquiry-status-filter`.
- Button per inquiry `delete-inquiry-button-{inquiry_id}`.

### 4.7 Favorites Page
- Container div `favorites-list`.
- List favorite properties with buttons:
  - `remove-from-favorites-button-{property_id}`
  - `view-property-button-{property_id}`
- Back button `back-to-dashboard`.

### 4.8 Agents Page
- Container div `agents-list`.
- List agents with contact button `contact-agent-button-{agent_id}`.
- Back button `back-to-dashboard`.

### 4.9 Locations Page
- Container `locations-page`.
- List locations with summary info.
- Buttons `view-location-button-{location_id}` for viewing location details.
- Sort dropdown by average price `location-sort-dropdown`.
- Back to dashboard button.

---

## 5. Data File Schemas

### 5.1 Properties (`properties.txt`)
Format:
```
property_id|address|location|price|property_type|bedrooms|bathrooms|square_feet|description|agent_id|status
```

### 5.2 Locations (`locations.txt`)
Format:
```
location_id|location_name|region|average_price|property_count|description
```

### 5.3 Inquiries (`inquiries.txt`)
Format:
```
inquiry_id|property_id|customer_name|customer_email|customer_phone|message|inquiry_date|status
```

### 5.4 Favorites (`favorites.txt`)
Format:
```
favorite_id|property_id|added_date
```

### 5.5 Agents (`agents.txt`)
Format:
```
agent_id|name|agency|email|phone|specialization
```

---

## 6. Development Notes
- Use Flask routing to map URLs to functions rendering templates with correct context.
- Utilize Jinja2 for template rendering with dynamic elements.
- Load and save data from/to text files with locking to handle concurrency.
- Maintain consistent ID keys for properties, inquiries, agents, etc.
- Ensure navigation links are consistent across all pages.
- No database or external services are used.
- Implement clear error handling for file I/O issues.
- Modularize code for maintainability.

Buttons to view location properties. - Context Variables:   - `locations` - list of location dicts  ---  ## 4. HTML Templates Outline  ### 4.1 Base Layout - Navigation menu with links to Dashboard, Search, Favorites, Inquiries, Agents, Locations.  ### 4.2 Dashboard Page - Container div with id `dashboard-container`. - Section showing featured properties each with button linking to property details. - Buttons:   - `browse-properties-button` - navigates to search.   - `my-favorites-button` - navigates to favorites page.  ### 4.3 Search Page - Search form with input fields:   - `price-range-min` (number input)   - `price-range-max` (number input)   - `property-type-filter` (dropdown)   - `location-filter` (dropdown) - Search results displayed as property cards. - Each card contains:   - Image, address, price, bedrooms, bathrooms.   - Button linking to property details.  ### 4.4 Property Details Page - Container div `property-details-page`. - Display property price `property-price`. - Description div `property-description`. - Button `add-favorite-button` to add property to favorites. - Button `submit-inquiry-button` to open inquiry form.  ### 4.5 Inquiry Form Page - Container `inquiry-page`. - Form inputs:   - `inquiry-name` (text)   - `inquiry-email` (email)   - `inquiry-phone` (tel)   - `inquiry-message` (textarea)   - Dropdown to select property if inquiry is general. - Submit button `submit-inquiry-button`.  ### 4.6 Inquiries List Page - Container `inquiries-page`. - Table `inquiries-table` listing inquiries with columns for property, customer, date, and status. - Dropdown filter `inquiry-status-filter`. - Button per inquiry `delete-inquiry-button-{inquiry_id}`.  ### 4.7 Favorites Page - Container div `favorites-list`. - List favorite properties with buttons:   - `remove-from-favorites-button-{property_id}`   - `view-property-button-{property_id}` - Back button `back-to-dashboard`.  ### 4.8 Agents Page - Container div `agents-list`. - List agents with contact button `contact-agent-button-{agent_id}`. - Back button `back-to-dashboard`.  ### 4.9 Locations Page - Container `locations-page`. - List locations with summary info. - Buttons `view-location-button-{location_id}` for viewing location details. - Sort dropdown by average price `location-sort-dropdown`. - Back to dashboard button.  ---  ## 5. Data File Schemas  ### 5.1 Properties (`properties.txt`) Format: ``` property_id|address|location|price|property_type|bedrooms|bathrooms|square_feet|description|agent_id|status ```  ### 5.2 Locations (`locations.txt`) Format: ``` location_id|location_name|region|average_price|property_count|description ```  ### 5.3 Inquiries (`inquiries.txt`) Format: ``` inquiry_id|property_id|customer_name|customer_email|customer_phone|message|inquiry_date|status ```  ### 5.4 Favorites (`favorites.txt`) Format: ``` favorite_id|property_id|added_date ```  ### 5.5 Agents (`agents.txt`) Format: ``` agent_id|name|agency|email|phone|specialization ```  ---  ## 6. Development Notes - Use Flask routing to map URLs to functions rendering templates with correct context. - Utilize Jinja2 for template rendering with dynamic elements. - Load and save data from/to text files with locking to handle concurrency. - Maintain consistent ID keys for properties, inquiries, agents, etc. - Ensure navigation links are consistent across all pages. - No database or external services are used. - Implement clear error handling for file I/O issues. - Modularize code for maintainability.

# Requirements Document for 'RealEstate' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'RealEstate' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse property listings, search by location and price, view property details, submit inquiries, and manage favorite properties. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'RealEstate' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'RealEstate' web application will consist of the following eight pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Real Estate Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured properties, recent listings, and quick navigation to all functionalities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: featured-properties** - Type: Div - Display of featured property recommendations.
  - **ID: browse-properties-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to property search page.
  - **ID: my-inquiries-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to inquiries page.
  - **ID: my-favorites-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to favorites page.

### 2. Property Search Page
- **Page Title**: Property Search
- **Overview**: A page displaying all available properties with advanced search and filter capabilities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: search-page** - Type: Div - Container for the search page.
  - **ID: location-input** - Type: Input - Field to search properties by location/city.
  - **ID: price-range-min** - Type: Input (number) - Field to set minimum price filter.
  - **ID: price-range-max** - Type: Input (number) - Field to set maximum price filter.
  - **ID: property-type-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by property type (House, Apartment, Condo, Land).
  - **ID: properties-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying property cards with image, location, price, and beds/baths.
  - **ID: view-property-button-{property_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view property details (each property card has this).

### 3. Property Details Page
- **Page Title**: Property Details
- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific property.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: property-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the property details page.
  - **ID: property-address** - Type: H1 - Display property address.
  - **ID: property-price** - Type: Div - Display property price.
  - **ID: property-description** - Type: Div - Display property description.
  - **ID: property-features** - Type: Div - Display property features (beds, baths, square footage).
  - **ID: add-to-favorites-button** - Type: Button - Button to add property to favorites.
  - **ID: submit-inquiry-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit inquiry for property.

### 4. Property Inquiry Page
- **Page Title**: Submit Property Inquiry
- **Overview**: A page for users to submit inquiries for properties they are interested in.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: inquiry-page** - Type: Div - Container for the inquiry page.
  - **ID: select-property** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select property for inquiry.
  - **ID: inquiry-name** - Type: Input - Field to input customer name.
  - **ID: inquiry-email** - Type: Input (email) - Field to input customer email.
  - **ID: inquiry-phone** - Type: Input (tel) - Field to input customer phone.
  - **ID: inquiry-message** - Type: Textarea - Field to write inquiry message.
  - **ID: submit-inquiry-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit inquiry.

### 5. My Inquiries Page
- **Page Title**: My Inquiries
- **Overview**: A page displaying all submitted inquiries and their status.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: inquiries-page** - Type: Div - Container for the inquiries page.
  - **ID: inquiries-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying inquiries with property, date, status, and contact info.
  - **ID: inquiry-status-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (All, Pending, Contacted, Resolved).
  - **ID: delete-inquiry-button-{inquiry_id}** - Type: Button - Button to delete inquiry (each inquiry has this).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 6. My Favorites Page
- **Page Title**: My Favorite Properties
- **Overview**: A page displaying all properties added to favorites.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: favorites-page** - Type: Div - Container for the favorites page.
  - **ID: favorites-list** - Type: Div - List of all favorite properties with address, price, and action buttons.
  - **ID: remove-from-favorites-button-{property_id}** - Type: Button - Button to remove property from favorites (each property has this).
  - **ID: view-property-button-{property_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view property details (each property has this).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 7. Agent Directory Page
- **Page Title**: Real Estate Agents
- **Overview**: A page displaying all real estate agents and their contact information.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: agents-page** - Type: Div - Container for the agents page.
  - **ID: agents-list** - Type: Div - List of all agents with photo, name, specialization, and contact info.
  - **ID: agent-search** - Type: Input - Field to search agents by name.
  - **ID: contact-agent-button-{agent_id}** - Type: Button - Button to contact agent (each agent has this).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 8. Locations Page
- **Page Title**: Featured Locations
- **Overview**: A page displaying popular locations with property count and details.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: locations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the locations page.
  - **ID: locations-list** - Type: Div - List of all locations with name, property count, and average price.
  - **ID: view-location-button-{location_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view properties in location (each location has this).
  - **ID: location-sort** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to sort locations (By Name, By Properties Count, By Average Price).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'RealEstate' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. Properties Data
- **File Name**: `properties.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  property_id|address|location|price|property_type|bedrooms|bathrooms|square_feet|description|agent_id|status
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|123 Oak Street|Downtown|450000|House|3|2|2500|Beautiful family home with large yard|101|Available
  2|456 Park Avenue|Midtown|350000|Apartment|2|1.5|1200|Modern apartment with city view|102|Available
  3|789 Elm Road|Suburb|280000|Condo|2|2|1500|Cozy condo in quiet neighborhood|101|Sold
  ```

### 2. Locations Data
- **File Name**: `locations.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  location_id|location_name|region|average_price|property_count|description
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Downtown|Central|425000|45|Urban area with business district
  2|Midtown|Central|380000|38|Mixed residential and commercial zone
  3|Suburb|Outskirts|295000|52|Family-friendly residential area
  ```

### 3. Property Inquiries Data
- **File Name**: `inquiries.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  inquiry_id|property_id|customer_name|customer_email|customer_phone|message|inquiry_date|status
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|John Smith|john@email.com|555-1234|Interested in viewing this weekend|2025-01-15|Pending
  2|2|Sarah Johnson|sarah@email.com|555-5678|Can we schedule a showing?|2025-01-16|Contacted
  3|1|Mike Davis|mike@email.com|555-9012|What is the lowest offer?|2025-01-17|Resolved
  ```

### 4. Favorite Properties Data
- **File Name**: `favorites.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  favorite_id|property_id|added_date
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|2025-01-10
  2|2|2025-01-12
  3|3|2025-01-14
  ```

### 5. Real Estate Agents Data
- **File Name**: `agents.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  agent_id|agent_name|specialization|email|phone|properties_sold
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  101|Robert Wilson|Residential Properties|robert@email.com|555-0001|125
  102|Emily Chen|Commercial Real Estate|emily@email.com|555-0002|89
  103|James Martinez|Luxury Homes|james@email.com|555-0003|67
  ```


=== design_spec.md ===
# RealEstate Application Design Specification

## 1. Objective

Develop a comprehensive design specification for a fully functional local file-based RealEstate web application where users can browse property listings, search by location and price, view property details, submit property inquiries, and manage favorite properties. Entirely based on Python Flask backend with local text file data storage.

## 2. Technology Stack
- Backend: Python with Flask
- Frontend: HTML5 with Jinja2 templating
- Data Storage: Local text files

---

## 3. Flask Routes Specification

### 3.1 Dashboard
- URL: `/`
- Methods: GET
- Description: Main landing page showing featured properties, navigation links to search, favorites, inquiries, agents, and locations.
- Context Variables:
  - `featured_properties` - list of featured property dicts

---

### 3.2 Search Properties
- URL: `/search`
- Methods: GET, POST
- Description: Page with search form to filter properties by price range (min/max), property type, location.
- Context Variables:
  - `properties` - list of filtered property dicts
  - `filters` - dict of submitted filter criteria

---

### 3.3 Property Details
- URL: `/property/<property_id>`
- Methods: GET
- Description: Display detailed property information, with buttons to add to favorites and submit inquiry.
- Context Variables:
  - `property` - dict of property details

---

### 3.4 Submit Inquiry
- URL: `/inquiry` or `/inquiry/<property_id>`
- Methods: GET, POST
- Description: Form page to submit an inquiry about a property or a general inquiry.
- Context Variables:
  - `property` (optional) - dict of property details

---

### 3.5 View Inquiries
- URL: `/inquiries`
- Methods: GET
- Description: List all submitted inquiries with filter by status.
- Context Variables:
  - `inquiries` - list of inquiry dicts
  - `status_filter` - current filter status

---

### 3.6 Favorites Page
- URL: `/favorites`
- Methods: GET
- Description: Displays favorite properties, with buttons to remove favorites and view property details.
- Context Variables:
  - `favorites` - list of favorite property dicts

---

### 3.7 Agents Page
- URL: `/agents`
- Methods: GET
- Description: List all real estate agents with contact buttons.
- Context Variables:
  - `agents` - list of agents dicts

---

### 3.8 Locations Page
- URL: `/locations`
- Methods: GET
- Description: List locations with average price and counts. Buttons to view location properties.
- Context Variables:
  - `locations` - list of location dicts

---

## 4. HTML Templates Outline

### 4.1 Base Layout
- Navigation menu with links to Dashboard, Search, Favorites, Inquiries, Agents, Locations.

### 4.2 Dashboard Page
- Container div with id `dashboard-container`.
- Section showing featured properties each with button linking to property details.
- Buttons:
  - `browse-properties-button` - navigates to search.
  - `my-favorites-button` - navigates to favorites page.

### 4.3 Search Page
- Search form with input fields:
  - `price-range-min` (number input)
  - `price-range-max` (number input)
  - `property-type-filter` (dropdown)
  - `location-filter` (dropdown)
- Search results displayed as property cards.
- Each card contains:
  - Image, address, price, bedrooms, bathrooms.
  - Button linking to property details.

### 4.4 Property Details Page
- Container div `property-details-page`.
- Display property price `property-price`.
- Description div `property-description`.
- Button `add-favorite-button` to add property to favorites.
- Button `submit-inquiry-button` to open inquiry form.

### 4.5 Inquiry Form Page
- Container `inquiry-page`.
- Form inputs:
  - `inquiry-name` (text)
  - `inquiry-email` (email)
  - `inquiry-phone` (tel)
  - `inquiry-message` (textarea)
  - Dropdown to select property if inquiry is general.
- Submit button `submit-inquiry-button`.

### 4.6 Inquiries List Page
- Container `inquiries-page`.
- Table `inquiries-table` listing inquiries with columns for property, customer, date, and status.
- Dropdown filter `inquiry-status-filter`.
- Button per inquiry `delete-inquiry-button-{inquiry_id}`.

### 4.7 Favorites Page
- Container div `favorites-list`.
- List favorite properties with buttons:
  - `remove-from-favorites-button-{property_id}`
  - `view-property-button-{property_id}`
- Back button `back-to-dashboard`.

### 4.8 Agents Page
- Container div `agents-list`.
- List agents with contact button `contact-agent-button-{agent_id}`.
- Back button `back-to-dashboard`.

### 4.9 Locations Page
- Container `locations-page`.
- List locations with summary info.
- Buttons `view-location-button-{location_id}` for viewing location details.
- Sort dropdown by average price `location-sort-dropdown`.
- Back to dashboard button.

---

## 5. Data File Schemas

### 5.1 Properties (`properties.txt`)
Format:
```
property_id|address|location|price|property_type|bedrooms|bathrooms|square_feet|description|agent_id|status
```

### 5.2 Locations (`locations.txt`)
Format:
```
location_id|location_name|region|average_price|property_count|description
```

### 5.3 Inquiries (`inquiries.txt`)
Format:
```
inquiry_id|property_id|customer_name|customer_email|customer_phone|message|inquiry_date|status
```

### 5.4 Favorites (`favorites.txt`)
Format:
```
favorite_id|property_id|added_date
```

### 5.5 Agents (`agents.txt`)
Format:
```
agent_id|name|agency|email|phone|specialization
```

---

## 6. Development Notes
- Use Flask routing to map URLs to functions rendering templates with correct context.
- Utilize Jinja2 for template rendering with dynamic elements.
- Load and save data from/to text files with locking to handle concurrency.
- Maintain consistent ID keys for properties, inquiries, agents, etc.
- Ensure navigation links are consistent across all pages.
- No database or external services are used.
- Implement clear error handling for file I/O issues.
- Modularize code for maintainability.

# Requirements Document for 'RealEstate' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'RealEstate' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse property listings, search by location and price, view property details, submit inquiries, and manage favorite properties. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'RealEstate' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'RealEstate' web application will consist of the following eight pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Real Estate Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured properties, recent listings, and quick navigation to all functionalities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: featured-properties** - Type: Div - Display of featured property recommendations.
  - **ID: browse-properties-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to property search page.
  - **ID: my-inquiries-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to inquiries page.
  - **ID: my-favorites-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to favorites page.

### 2. Property Search Page
- **Page Title**: Property Search
- **Overview**: A page displaying all available properties with advanced search and filter capabilities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: search-page** - Type: Div - Container for the search page.
  - **ID: location-input** - Type: Input - Field to search properties by location/city.
  - **ID: price-range-min** - Type: Input (number) - Field to set minimum price filter.
  - **ID: price-range-max** - Type: Input (number) - Field to set maximum price filter.
  - **ID: property-type-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by property type (House, Apartment, Condo, Land).
  - **ID: properties-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying property cards with image, location, price, and beds/baths.
  - **ID: view-property-button-{property_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view property details (each property card has this).

### 3. Property Details Page
- **Page Title**: Property Details
- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific property.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: property-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the property details page.
  - **ID: property-address** - Type: H1 - Display property address.
  - **ID: property-price** - Type: Div - Display property price.
  - **ID: property-description** - Type: Div - Display property description.
  - **ID: property-features** - Type: Div - Display property features (beds, baths, square footage).
  - **ID: add-to-favorites-button** - Type: Button - Button to add property to favorites.
  - **ID: submit-inquiry-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit inquiry for property.

### 4. Property Inquiry Page
- **Page Title**: Submit Property Inquiry
- **Overview**: A page for users to submit inquiries for properties they are interested in.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: inquiry-page** - Type: Div - Container for the inquiry page.
  - **ID: select-property** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select property for inquiry.
  - **ID: inquiry-name** - Type: Input - Field to input customer name.
  - **ID: inquiry-email** - Type: Input (email) - Field to input customer email.
  - **ID: inquiry-phone** - Type: Input (tel) - Field to input customer phone.
  - **ID: inquiry-message** - Type: Textarea - Field to write inquiry message.
  - **ID: submit-inquiry-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit inquiry.

### 5. My Inquiries Page
- **Page Title**: My Inquiries
- **Overview**: A page displaying all submitted inquiries and their status.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: inquiries-page** - Type: Div - Container for the inquiries page.
  - **ID: inquiries-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying inquiries with property, date, status, and contact info.
  - **ID: inquiry-status-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (All, Pending, Contacted, Resolved).
  - **ID: delete-inquiry-button-{inquiry_id}** - Type: Button - Button to delete inquiry (each inquiry has this).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 6. My Favorites Page
- **Page Title**: My Favorite Properties
- **Overview**: A page displaying all properties added to favorites.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: favorites-page** - Type: Div - Container for the favorites page.
  - **ID: favorites-list** - Type: Div - List of all favorite properties with address, price, and action buttons.
  - **ID: remove-from-favorites-button-{property_id}** - Type: Button - Button to remove property from favorites (each property has this).
  - **ID: view-property-button-{property_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view property details (each property has this).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 7. Agent Directory Page
- **Page Title**: Real Estate Agents
- **Overview**: A page displaying all real estate agents and their contact information.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: agents-page** - Type: Div - Container for the agents page.
  - **ID: agents-list** - Type: Div - List of all agents with photo, name, specialization, and contact info.
  - **ID: agent-search** - Type: Input - Field to search agents by name.
  - **ID: contact-agent-button-{agent_id}** - Type: Button - Button to contact agent (each agent has this).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 8. Locations Page
- **Page Title**: Featured Locations
- **Overview**: A page displaying popular locations with property count and details.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: locations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the locations page.
  - **ID: locations-list** - Type: Div - List of all locations with name, property count, and average price.
  - **ID: view-location-button-{location_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view properties in location (each location has this).
  - **ID: location-sort** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to sort locations (By Name, By Properties Count, By Average Price).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'RealEstate' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. Properties Data
- **File Name**: `properties.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  property_id|address|location|price|property_type|bedrooms|bathrooms|square_feet|description|agent_id|status
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|123 Oak Street|Downtown|450000|House|3|2|2500|Beautiful family home with large yard|101|Available
  2|456 Park Avenue|Midtown|350000|Apartment|2|1.5|1200|Modern apartment with city view|102|Available
  3|789 Elm Road|Suburb|280000|Condo|2|2|1500|Cozy condo in quiet neighborhood|101|Sold
  ```

### 2. Locations Data
- **File Name**: `locations.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  location_id|location_name|region|average_price|property_count|description
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Downtown|Central|425000|45|Urban area with business district
  2|Midtown|Central|380000|38|Mixed residential and commercial zone
  3|Suburb|Outskirts|295000|52|Family-friendly residential area
  ```

### 3. Property Inquiries Data
- **File Name**: `inquiries.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  inquiry_id|property_id|customer_name|customer_email|customer_phone|message|inquiry_date|status
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|John Smith|john@email.com|555-1234|Interested in viewing this weekend|2025-01-15|Pending
  2|2|Sarah Johnson|sarah@email.com|555-5678|Can we schedule a showing?|2025-01-16|Contacted
  3|1|Mike Davis|mike@email.com|555-9012|What is the lowest offer?|2025-01-17|Resolved
  ```

### 4. Favorite Properties Data
- **File Name**: `favorites.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  favorite_id|property_id|added_date
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|2025-01-10
  2|2|2025-01-12
  3|3|2025-01-14
  ```

### 5. Real Estate Agents Data
- **File Name**: `agents.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  agent_id|agent_name|specialization|email|phone|properties_sold
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  101|Robert Wilson|Residential Properties|robert@email.com|555-0001|125
  102|Emily Chen|Commercial Real Estate|emily@email.com|555-0002|89
  103|James Martinez|Luxury Homes|james@email.com|555-0003|67
  ```

Favorite Properties Data - **File Name**: `favorites.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   favorite_id|property_id|added_date   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|2025-01-10   2|2|2025-01-12   3|3|2025-01-14   ```  ### 5. Property Inquiry Page - **Page Title**: Submit Property Inquiry - **Overview**: A page for users to submit inquiries for properties they are interested in. - **Elements**:   - **ID: inquiry-page** - Type: Div - Container for the inquiry page.   - **ID: select-property** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select property for inquiry.   - **ID: inquiry-name** - Type: Input - Field to input customer name.   - **ID: inquiry-email** - Type: Input (email) - Field to input customer email.   - **ID: inquiry-phone** - Type: Input (tel) - Field to input customer phone.   - **ID: inquiry-message** - Type: Textarea - Field to write inquiry message.   - **ID: submit-inquiry-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit inquiry.  ### 5. My Inquiries Page - **Page Title**: My Inquiries - **Overview**: A page displaying all submitted inquiries and their status. - **Elements**:   - **ID: inquiries-page** - Type: Div - Container for the inquiries page.   - **ID: inquiries-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying inquiries with property, date, status, and contact info.   - **ID: inquiry-status-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (All, Pending, Contacted, Resolved).   - **ID: delete-inquiry-button-{inquiry_id}** - Type: Button - Button to delete inquiry (each inquiry has this).   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 6. My Favorites Page - **Page Title**: My Favorite Properties - **Overview**: A page displaying all properties added to favorites. - **Elements**:   - **ID: favorites-page** - Type: Div - Container for the favorites page.   - **ID: favorites-list** - Type: Div - List of all favorite properties with address, price, and action buttons.   - **ID: remove-from-favorites-button-{property_id}** - Type: Button - Button to remove property from favorites (each property has this).   - **ID: view-property-button-{property_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view property details (each property has this).   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 7. Agent Directory Page - **Page Title**: Real Estate Agents - **Overview**: A page displaying all real estate agents and their contact information. - **Elements**:   - **ID: agents-page** - Type: Div - Container for the agents page.   - **ID: agents-list** - Type: Div - List of all agents with photo, name, specialization, and contact info.   - **ID: agent-search** - Type: Input - Field to search agents by name.   - **ID: contact-agent-button-{agent_id}** - Type: Button - Button to contact agent (each agent has this).   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 8. Locations Page - **Page Title**: Featured Locations - **Overview**: A page displaying popular locations with property count and details. - **Elements**:   - **ID: locations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the locations page.   - **ID: locations-list** - Type: Div - List of all locations with name, property count, and average price.   - **ID: view-location-button-{location_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view properties in location (each location has this).   - **ID: location-sort** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to sort locations (By Name, By Properties Count, By Average Price).   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ## 4. Data Storage  The 'RealEstate' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:  ### 1. Properties Data - **File Name**: `properties.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   property_id|address|location|price|property_type|bedrooms|bathrooms|square_feet|description|agent_id|status   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|123 Oak Street|Downtown|450000|House|3|2|2500|Beautiful family home with large yard|101|Available   2|456 Park Avenue|Midtown|350000|Apartment|2|1.5|1200|Modern apartment with city view|102|Available   3|789 Elm Road|Suburb|280000|Condo|2|2|1500|Cozy condo in quiet neighborhood|101|Sold   ```  ### 2. Locations Data - **File Name**: `locations.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   location_id|location_name|region|average_price|property_count|description   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Downtown|Central|425000|45|Urban area with business district   2|Midtown|Central|380000|38|Mixed residential and commercial zone   3|Suburb|Outskirts|295000|52|Family-friendly residential area   ```  ### 3. Property Inquiries Data - **File Name**: `inquiries.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   inquiry_id|property_id|customer_name|customer_email|customer_phone|message|inquiry_date|status   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|John Smith|john@email.com|555-1234|Interested in viewing this weekend|2025-01-15|Pending   2|2|Sarah Johnson|sarah@email.com|555-5678|Can we schedule a showing?|2025-01-16|Contacted   3|1|Mike Davis|mike@email.com|555-9012|What is the lowest offer?|2025-01-17|Resolved   ```  ### 4. Favorite Properties Data - **File Name**: `favorites.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   favorite_id|property_id|added_date   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|1|2025-01-10   2|2|2025-01-12   3|3|2025-01-14   ```  ### 5. Real Estate Agents Data - **File Name**: `agents.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   agent_id|agent_name|specialization|email|phone|properties_sold   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   101|Robert Wilson|Residential Properties|robert@email.com|555-0001|125   102|Emily Chen|Commercial Real Estate|emily@email.com|555-0002|89   103|James Martinez|Luxury Homes|james@email.com|555-0003|67   ```
  [design_spec.md] # RealEstate Flask Web Application Design Specification  ---  ## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification (Backend Focus)  ### Route 1: Dashboard - URL Path: `/` - HTTP Methods: `GET` - Function Name: `dashboard` - Behavior: Redirects root URL `/` to dashboard page `/dashboard`.  ### Route 2: Dashboard Page - URL Path: `/dashboard` - HTTP Methods: `GET` - Function Name: `dashboard_page` - HTML Template: `dashboard.html` - Context Variables:   - `featured_properties` (list of dict): List of featured properties each dict containing: `property_id` (str), `address` (str), `price` (float), `property_type` (str), `bedrooms` (int), `bathrooms` (float), `square_feet` (int), `description` (str) - Form Data: None  ### Route 3: Property Search - URL Path: `/search` - HTTP Methods: `GET`, `POST` - Function Name: `property_search` - HTML Template: `search.html` - Context Variables:   - `properties` (list of dict): List of filtered properties with same fields as featured_properties   - `filters` (dict): Search filters including keys - `location` (str), `price_min` (float), `price_max` (float), `property_type` (str) - Form Data (POST):   - `location` (str): Input location or city to filter   - `price_min` (float): Minimum price filter   - `price_max` (float): Maximum price filter   - `property_type` (str): Property type filter (House, Apartment, Condo, Land)  ### Route 4: Property Details - URL Path: `/property/<property_id>` - HTTP Methods: `GET` - Function Name: `property_details` - HTML Template: `property_details.html` - Route Parameters:   - `property_id` (str): Identifier of the property to view - Context Variables:   - `property` (dict): Property details including fields:     - `property_id` (str)     - `address` (str)     - `location` (str)     - `price` (float)     - `property_type` (str)     - `bedrooms` (int)     - `bathrooms` (float)     - `square_feet` (int)     - `description` (str)     - `agent_id` (str)     - `status` (str) - Form Data: None  ### Route 5: Property Inquiry - URL Path: `/inquiry` - HTTP Methods: `GET`, `POST` - Function Name: `property_inquiry` - HTML Template: `inquiry.html` - Context Variables:   - `properties` (list of dict): List of all properties for selection - Form Data (POST):   - `selected_property` (str): Property ID selected for inquiry   - `inquiry_name` (str): Customer name   - `inquiry_email` (str): Customer email   - `inquiry_phone` (str): Customer phone   - `inquiry_message` (str): Message content  ### Route 6: My Inquiries - URL Path: `/inquiries` - HTTP Methods: `GET` - Function Name: `my_inquiries` - HTML Template: `inquiries.html` - Context Variables:   - `inquiries` (list of dict): List of inquiries with fields:     - `inquiry_id` (str)     - `property_id` (str)     - `property_address` (str)     - `customer_name` (str)     - `customer_email` (str)     - `customer_phone` (str)     - `message` (str)     - `inquiry_date` (str, date in YYYY-MM-DD format)     - `status` (str)   - `status_filter` (str): Current filter status (All, Pending, Contacted, Resolved) - Form Data: None  ### Route 7: My Favorites - URL Path: `/favorites` - HTTP Methods: `GET` - Function Name: `my_favorites` - HTML Template: `favorites.html` - Context Variables:   - `favorites` (list of dict): List of favorite properties with fields matching properties - Form Data: None  ### Route 8: Agent Directory - URL Path: `/agents` - HTTP Methods: `GET` - Function Name: `agent_directory` - HTML Template: `agents.html` - Context Variables:   - `agents` (list of dict): List of agents with fields:     - `agent_id` (str)     - `agent_name` (str)     - `specialization` (str)     - `email` (str)     - `phone` (str)     - `properties_sold` (int) - Form Data: None  ### Route 9: Locations Page - URL Path: `/locations` - HTTP Methods: `GET` - Function Name: `locations_page` - HTML Template: `locations.html` - Context Variables:   - `locations` (list of dict): List of locations with fields:     - `location_id` (str)     - `location_name` (str)     - `region` (str)     - `average_price` (float)     - `property_count` (int)     - `description` (str) - Form Data: None  ---  ## Section 2: HTML Templates Specification (Frontend Focus)  ### dashboard.html - Page Title: Real Estate Dashboard - Element IDs:   - File Path: `data/properties.txt` - Fields (pipe-delimited):   - `property_id` (str): Unique property identifier   - `address` (str): Property address   - `location` (str): Location or city   - `price` (float): Property price   - `property_type` (str): Type of property (House, Apartment, Condo, Land)   - `bedrooms` (int): Number of bedrooms   - `bathrooms` (float): Number of bathrooms (can be fractional e.g., 1.5)   - `square_feet` (int): Square footage   - `description` (str): Property description   - `agent_id` (str): Associated agent ID   - `status` (str): Property status (Available, Sold, etc.) - Example Rows: ``` 1|123 Oak Street|Downtown|450000|House|3|2|2500|Beautiful family home with large yard|101|Available 2|456 Park Avenue|Midtown|350000|Apartment|2|1.5|1200|Modern apartment with city view|102|Available 3|789 Elm Road|Suburb|280000|Condo|2|2|1500|Cozy condo in quiet neighborhood|101|Sold ```  ### 3.2 locations.txt - File Path: `data/locations.txt` - Fields (pipe-delimited):   - `location_id` (str): Unique location identifier   - `location_name` (str): Name of location   - `region` (str): Geographic region   - `average_price` (float): Average property price   - `property_count` (int): Number of properties in location   - `description` (str): Location description - Example Rows: ``` 1|Downtown|Central|425000|45|Urban area with business district 2|Midtown|Central|380000|38|Mixed residential and commercial zone 3|Suburb|Outskirts|295000|52|Family-friendly residential area ```  ### 3.3 inquiries.txt - File Path: `data/inquiries.txt` - Fields (pipe-delimited):   - `inquiry_id` (str): Unique inquiry identifier   - `property_id` (str): Associated property ID   - `customer_name` (str): Customer full name   - `customer_email` (str): Customer email   - `customer_phone` (str): Customer phone number   - `message` (str): Inquiry message content   - `inquiry_date` (str): Date of inquiry (YYYY-MM-DD)   - `status` (str): Status of inquiry (Pending, Contacted, Resolved) - Example Rows: ``` 1|1|John Smith|john@email.com|555-1234|Interested in viewing this weekend|2025-01-15|Pending 2|2|Sarah Johnson|sarah@email.com|555-5678|Can we schedule a showing?|2025-01-16|Contacted 3|1|Mike Davis|mike@email.com|555-9012|What is the lowest offer?|2025-01-17|Resolved ```  ### 3.4 favorites.txt - File Path: `data/favorites.txt` - Fields (pipe-delimited):   - `favorite_id` (str): Unique favorite entry ID   - `property_id` (str): Favorited property ID   - `added_date` (str): Date added (YYYY-MM-DD) - Example Rows: ``` 1|1|2025-01-10 2|2|2025-01-12 3|3|2025-01-14 ```  ### 3.5 agents.txt - File Path: `data/agents.txt` - Fields (pipe-delimited):   - `agent_id` (str): Unique agent identifier   - `agent_name` (str): Full name of agent   - `specialization` (str): Agent's area of expertise   - `email` (str): Agent email   - `phone` (str): Agent phone   - `properties_sold` (int): Number of properties sold - Example Rows: ``` 101|Robert Wilson|Residential Properties|robert@email.com|555-0001|125 102|Emily Chen|Commercial Real Estate|emily@email.com|555-0002|89 103|James Martinez|Luxury Homes|james@email.com|555-0003|67 ```

# Requirements Document for 'RealEstate' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'RealEstate' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse property listings, search by location and price, view property details, submit inquiries, and manage favorite properties. No authentication required - all features are directly accessible. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'RealEstate' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'RealEstate' web application will consist of the following eight pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Real Estate Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured properties, recent listings, and quick navigation to all functionalities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: featured-properties** - Type: Div - Display of featured property recommendations.
  - **ID: browse-properties-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to property search page.
  - **ID: my-inquiries-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to inquiries page.
  - **ID: my-favorites-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to favorites page.

### 2. Property Search Page
- **Page Title**: Property Search
- **Overview**: A page displaying all available properties with advanced search and filter capabilities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: search-page** - Type: Div - Container for the search page.
  - **ID: location-input** - Type: Input - Field to search properties by location/city.
  - **ID: price-range-min** - Type: Input (number) - Field to set minimum price filter.
  - **ID: price-range-max** - Type: Input (number) - Field to set maximum price filter.
  - **ID: property-type-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by property type (House, Apartment, Condo, Land).
  - **ID: properties-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying property cards with image, location, price, and beds/baths.
  - **ID: view-property-button-{property_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view property details (each property card has this).

### 3. Property Details Page
- **Page Title**: Property Details
- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific property.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: property-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the property details page.
  - **ID: property-address** - Type: H1 - Display property address.
  - **ID: property-price** - Type: Div - Display property price.
  - **ID: property-description** - Type: Div - Display property description.
  - **ID: property-features** - Type: Div - Display property features (beds, baths, square footage).
  - **ID: add-to-favorites-button** - Type: Button - Button to add property to favorites.
  - **ID: submit-inquiry-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit inquiry for property.

### 4. Property Inquiry Page
- **Page Title**: Submit Property Inquiry
- **Overview**: A page for users to submit inquiries for properties they are interested in.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: inquiry-page** - Type: Div - Container for the inquiry page.
  - **ID: select-property** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select property for inquiry.
  - **ID: inquiry-name** - Type: Input - Field to input customer name.
  - **ID: inquiry-email** - Type: Input (email) - Field to input customer email.
  - **ID: inquiry-phone** - Type: Input (tel) - Field to input customer phone.
  - **ID: inquiry-message** - Type: Textarea - Field to write inquiry message.
  - **ID: submit-inquiry-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit inquiry.

### 5. My Inquiries Page
- **Page Title**: My Inquiries
- **Overview**: A page displaying all submitted inquiries and their status.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: inquiries-page** - Type: Div - Container for the inquiries page.
  - **ID: inquiries-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying inquiries with property, date, status, and contact info.
  - **ID: inquiry-status-filter** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (All, Pending, Contacted, Resolved).
  - **ID: delete-inquiry-button-{inquiry_id}** - Type: Button - Button to delete inquiry (each inquiry has this).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 6. My Favorites Page
- **Page Title**: My Favorite Properties
- **Overview**: A page displaying all properties added to favorites.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: favorites-page** - Type: Div - Container for the favorites page.
  - **ID: favorites-list** - Type: Div - List of all favorite properties with address, price, and action buttons.
  - **ID: remove-from-favorites-button-{property_id}** - Type: Button - Button to remove property from favorites (each property has this).
  - **ID: view-property-button-{property_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view property details (each property has this).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 7. Agent Directory Page
- **Page Title**: Real Estate Agents
- **Overview**: A page displaying all real estate agents and their contact information.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: agents-page** - Type: Div - Container for the agents page.
  - **ID: agents-list** - Type: Div - List of all agents with photo, name, specialization, and contact info.
  - **ID: agent-search** - Type: Input - Field to search agents by name.
  - **ID: contact-agent-button-{agent_id}** - Type: Button - Button to contact agent (each agent has this).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 8. Locations Page
- **Page Title**: Featured Locations
- **Overview**: A page displaying popular locations with property count and details.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: locations-page** - Type: Div - Container for the locations page.
  - **ID: locations-list** - Type: Div - List of all locations with name, property count, and average price.
  - **ID: view-location-button-{location_id}** - Type: Button - Button to view properties in location (each location has this).
  - **ID: location-sort** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to sort locations (By Name, By Properties Count, By Average Price).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'RealEstate' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. Properties Data
- **File Name**: `properties.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  property_id|address|location|price|property_type|bedrooms|bathrooms|square_feet|description|agent_id|status
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|123 Oak Street|Downtown|450000|House|3|2|2500|Beautiful family home with large yard|101|Available
  2|456 Park Avenue|Midtown|350000|Apartment|2|1.5|1200|Modern apartment with city view|102|Available
  3|789 Elm Road|Suburb|280000|Condo|2|2|1500|Cozy condo in quiet neighborhood|101|Sold
  ```

### 2. Locations Data
- **File Name**: `locations.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  location_id|location_name|region|average_price|property_count|description
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Downtown|Central|425000|45|Urban area with business district
  2|Midtown|Central|380000|38|Mixed residential and commercial zone
  3|Suburb|Outskirts|295000|52|Family-friendly residential area
  ```

### 3. Property Inquiries Data
- **File Name**: `inquiries.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  inquiry_id|property_id|customer_name|customer_email|customer_phone|message|inquiry_date|status
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|John Smith|john@email.com|555-1234|Interested in viewing this weekend|2025-01-15|Pending
  2|2|Sarah Johnson|sarah@email.com|555-5678|Can we schedule a showing?|2025-01-16|Contacted
  3|1|Mike Davis|mike@email.com|555-9012|What is the lowest offer?|2025-01-17|Resolved
  ```

### 4. Favorite Properties Data
- **File Name**: `favorites.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  favorite_id|property_id|added_date
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|1|2025-01-10
  2|2|2025-01-12
  3|3|2025-01-14
  ```

### 5. Real Estate Agents Data
- **File Name**: `agents.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  agent_id|agent_name|specialization|email|phone|properties_sold
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  101|Robert Wilson|Residential Properties|robert@email.com|555-0001|125
  102|Emily Chen|Commercial Real Estate|emily@email.com|555-0002|89
  103|James Martinez|Luxury Homes|james@email.com|555-0003|67
  ```
